Only at note level (not paragraph level)
Hierarchical tags group by type and status
Used to define ExcaliBrain styles
Typifies the note:
- article
- video
- person
- meeting, etc. ^ymg9E2uW

Think of them as namespaces
Controls what gets synched with Obsidian
YouTube: starts with YYMMDD
Attachments subfolder is under folder
New files: same folder as current note ^n3OjGcOm

MoC:   _ (filename at the top of folder)
ICON:  Icon - keywords - Source
COVER: Book Cover - book title
IMAGE: Illustration - topic - Source
THUMBNAIL: Thumbnail - topic
Book on a Page: BoaP - Title
Literature Notes: LN - Title
Summary: Summary - Title
Date format YYYY-MM-DD
 ^fowdFc0i

Based on document tags (or vice versa)

Diagnostics and maintenance ^k9Lv1T6Q

Vault diagnostics
- Orphans
- "Pasted Image"  ^kt6CUcph

- Keep it simple: Each component has a clear purpose.
- Minimize friction: Automate to avoid clicking & typing.
- Brown-field reality: Accept what can't be changed
  easy: Archive-TheBrain, YouTube under Hobbies, etc.
- Avoid moving files around: Store notes where they
  were first created. Consequently some reference
  material might end up in a Project Folder, not the
  Input Folder and some attachments under Daily Notes.
- Apply LATCH: Maximize findability by building many paths
  to the same information. 
- ALWAYS link: create new items as a link, not just a file
  in a folder. ^pTRAPY46

Keep it simple
Minimize friction
Brown-field reality

Avoid moving files around



Apply LATCH

ALWAYS link: ^D7xKcEYA
